+++

Establishes the Oregon Right to Rest Act to protect individuals' rights to rest in public spaces, enforceable by the Commissioner of Bureau of Labor and Industries or through civil action.

[Original Bill Text](https://olis.oregonlegislature.gov/liz/2023R1/Measures/Overview/HB3501)

## Overview

Establishes Oregon Right to Rest Act. Makes violation unlawful practice enforceable by Commissioner of Bureau of Labor and Industries or by civil action. 
Takes effect on 91st day following adjournment sine die.
